Essential: bnj110.1


|- A e. _V

Essential: bnj110.2


|- ( ps <-> A. y e. A ( y R x -> [. y / x ]. ph ) )

Well-founded induction restricted to a set ( A e. _V ). The proof has been taken from Chapter 4 of Don Monk's notes on Set Theory. See ~ http://euclid.colorado.edu/~~monkd/setth.pdf . (Contributed by Jonathan Ben-Naim, 3-Jun-2011.) (New usage is discouraged.)

Theorem: bnj110


|- ( ( R Fr A /\ A. x e. A ( ps -> ph ) ) -> A. x e. A ph )
